case 'telkomsel-umum':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Umum'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©
 ï¼ˆËµâ€¢ ÖŠ â€¢Ëµ)â™¥ï¸Ž
â•­â”âˆªâ”âˆªâ”€â˜¾ *${catatanWaktu}* â˜½ËŠËŽ-

ðŸ›ï¸ *DATA TELKOMSEL*
  â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢à¸´.â€¢à¸´

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-bulk':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Bulk'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©
 ï¼ˆËµâ€¢ ÖŠ â€¢Ëµ)â™¥ï¸Ž
â•­â”âˆªâ”âˆªâ”€â˜¾ *${catatanWaktu}* â˜½ËŠËŽ-

ðŸ›ï¸ *DATA TELKOMSEL BULK*
  â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢à¸´.â€¢à¸´

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-flash':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Flash'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'

                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-mini':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Mini'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-vaganza':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Vaganza'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-maxstream':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Maxstream'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-umroh':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Umroh'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-malam':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Malam'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-combosakti':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Combo Sakti'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];

                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {

                        }

                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {

                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&

                                    item.type === 'GamesMAX Unlimited Play'
                            )

                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +

                            text: desk,

                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {

                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-youtube':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Youtube'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-instagram':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Instagram'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-facebook':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Facebook'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-ketengantiktok':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Ketengan TikTok'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }

case 'telkomsel-gamesmax':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'GamesMAX'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),

                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-musicmax':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'MusicMAX'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        });

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }

                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();

                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();

                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Disney+ Hotstar'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'

                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-omg':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'OMG'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-gigamax':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'GigaMAX'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-unlimitedmax':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'UnlimitedMAX'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'telkomsel-ilmupediaorbit':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Ilmupedia Orbit'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                            }));

                            )

                            .map((i) => ({

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
                
                
                
                
                
case 'telkomsel-surprisedeal':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Surprise Deal'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-ukm':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'UKM'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-ukmcombo':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'UKM COMBO'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-sumaterautarazona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumatera Utara Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-sumaterautarazona3':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumatera Utara Zona 3'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-sumateratengahzona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumatera Tengah Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-sumateratengahzona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumatera Tengah Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'

                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-sumateraselatanzona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumatera Selatan Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'telkomsel-bronze':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'TELKOMSEL' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Bronze'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
