                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       



//DATA INDOSAT
case 'indosat-umum':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Umum'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-giftdata':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Gift Data'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-yellow':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Yellow'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        });

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }

                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);

                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Freedom Combo'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin

                        });

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }

                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);

                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();

                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Freedom Internet Plus'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +

                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }

                }

                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);

                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();

                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();

                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Freedom Harian'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-mini':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Mini'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-freedominternet':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Freedom Internet'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-haji':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Haji'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-ekstra':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Ekstra'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-roaming':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Roaming'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-freedomu':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Freedom U'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        });

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }

                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);

                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();

                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();

                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Freedom Apps'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),

                        }));

                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({

                        });

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }

case 'indosat-yellowgift':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);

                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();

                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();

                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Yellow Gift'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-jabodetabek':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jabodetabek'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-jawabarat':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jawa Barat'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-jawatengah-diy':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jawa Tengah - DIY'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-kalimantanzona1:
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Kalimantan Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-kalimantanzona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Kalimantan Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-jawatengah-jawabarat':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jawa Tengah - Jawa Barat'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
case 'indosat-kalisumapa':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Kalisumapa'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }

case 'indosat-sumatera':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumatera'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
                
                
                
                
                
case 'indosat-ejbn':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'EJBN'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';

                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-freedomugift':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Freedom U Gift'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                            }));

                        });

                            text: desk,

                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {

                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {

                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&

                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({

                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }

case 'indosat-freedominternetgift':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);

                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();

                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Freedom Internet Gift'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +

                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {

                            )

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-jabodetabekzona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jabodetabek Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                            }));

                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {

                            )

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-jateng-diyzona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jateng - DIY Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-jabarzona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jabar Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-jabarzona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jabar Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-sumbagutzona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumbagut Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-sumbagutzona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumbagut Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'

                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-sumbagselzona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumbagsel Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
