                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-sumbagselzona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumbagsel Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-jatimzona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jatim Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-jatimzona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Jatim Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-balnuszona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Balnus Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-balnuszona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Balnus Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-sumapazona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumapa Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-sumapazona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumapa Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-sumaterazona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumatera Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-sumaterazona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumatera Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-umrohhajicombo':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Umroh Haji Combo'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-umrohhajiinternet':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Umroh Haji Internet'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-fifaworldcup':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'FIFA World Cup'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-freedommax':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Freedom Max'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-kalimantan':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Kalimantan'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-umkm':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'UMKM'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-kalisumapazona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Kalisumapa Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'

                        });

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }

                }

case 'indosat-extraboostergift':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);

                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();

                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();

                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Extra Booster Gift'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-Sumapa':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sumapa'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-gaspol':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'gaspol'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-Sachet':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Sachet'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-zona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-community':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Community'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-cwjzona1':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'CWJ Zona 1'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       
case 'indosat-cwjzona2':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'CWJ Zona 2'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;       

case 'indosat-puremerdeka':
                {
                    
                    if (konek.DF !== 'YA') {
                        m.reply(mess.maintenance);
                    } else {
                        const saldo = await koneksiDF.cekSaldoDF();
                        const cekSaldo = parseInt(saldo.deposit);
                        const listHarga = await koneksiDF.daftarHargaDF();
                        const list = listHarga
                            .filter(
                                (item) =>
                                    item.brand === 'INDOSAT' &&
                                    item.category === 'Data' &&
                                    item.type === 'Pure Merdeka'
                            )
                            .sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price)
                            .map((i) => ({
                                nama: i.product_name,
                                harga:
                                    i.price < 5000
                                        ? i.price + modals.markupMin
                                        : i.price +
                                          Math.ceil(i.price * modals.persen),
                                sku: i.buyer_sku_code,
                                stok:
                                    !i.seller_product_status
                                        ? 'Gangguan, hubungi owmer'
                                        : 'Tersedia',
                            }));
                        const judul = `â™¥ï¸Ž  âˆ©_._âˆ©

                        const isi = list.map((item) => {
                            const status =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan'
                                    : 'Tersedia';
                            const harga =
                                item.stok !== 'Tersedia'
                                    ? 'Gangguan, hubungi Owner'
                                    : rp(item.harga);
                            return `*${item.nama}*\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Harga :* ${harga}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Kode  :* ${item.sku}\n: Í€Ì—âž› *Info    :* ${status}\n\n`;
                        });

                        const caraPembelian = `â€¢â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â”â€¢`;

                        const desk = judul + isi.join('') + caraPembelian;

                        const desks = [desk, '*Cara Order*\nhttps://t.me/tutor_botdf/2'];
                        const messages = desks.map((desk) => ({
                            text: desk,
                            mentions: [sender],
                        }));
                        for (let i = 0; i < messages.length; i++) {
                            await vbot.sendMessage(from, messages[i]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                break;
